	#### SDAPO ####
	
	focus = {
		id = AUS_the_danubian_federation
		icon = GFX_goal_AUS_danubian_federation
		x = 5
		y = 10
		cost = 1.5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
			has_country_flag = AUS_SDAPO_WON
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = DNB_to_save_the_empire
		}
		completion_reward = {
			AUS_raise_govt_percentage_3 = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
	}
